scripted_gui = {

	#MILITARY CONTRACTS TOP BAR
	military_contracts = {
		window_name = military_contracts_main

		context_type = player
		parent_window_token = top_bar
		visible = {
			always = yes
		}

		effects = {
			military_contract_icon_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 1 }
					else = {
						set_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 0 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { original_tag = FRA }
					set_variable = { FRA_icons = 1 }
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = inf_eq_order_amount
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = h_inf_eq_order_amount
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = support_eq_order_amount
					value = 0
				}
			}
			military_contract_bg_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 1 }
					else = {
						set_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 0 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { original_tag = FRA }
					set_variable = { FRA_icons = 1 }
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = inf_eq_order_amount
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = h_inf_eq_order_amount
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = support_eq_order_amount
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}

			money_text_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { show_budget_tab = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { show_budget_tab = 1 }
					else = {
						set_variable = { show_budget_tab = 0 }
					}
				}
				# set_variable = {
				# 	var = gui_num_ships
				# 	value = num_ships
				# }
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_num_carriers
					value = num_ships_with_type@carrier
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_cost_of_carriers
					value = cost_of_carriers
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_num_battleship
					value = num_ships_with_type@battleship
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_cost_of_battleship
					value = cost_of_battleship
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_num_heavy_cruiser
					value = num_ships_with_type@heavy_cruiser
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_cost_of_heavy_cruiser
					value = cost_of_heavy_cruiser
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_num_light_cruiser
					value = num_ships_with_type@light_cruiser
				}

			money_bg_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { show_budget_tab = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { show_budget_tab = 1 }
					else = {
						set_variable = { show_budget_tab = 0 }
					}
				}
				# set_variable = {
				# 	var = gui_num_ships
				# 	value = num_ships
				# }
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_num_carriers
					value = num_ships_with_type@carrier
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_cost_of_carriers
					value = cost_of_carriers
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_num_battleship
					value = num_ships_with_type@battleship
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_cost_of_battleship
					value = cost_of_battleship
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_num_heavy_cruiser
					value = num_ships_with_type@heavy_cruiser
				}
				set_variable = {

					value = cost_of_heavy_cruiser
				}
				set_variable = {

				}

				}
				set_variable = {

					value = cost_of_destroyer
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_num_submarine

				}
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_cost_of_submarine
					value = cost_of_submarine
				}
				#Total navy cost
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_total_navy_cost
					value = 0
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = gui_total_navy_cost
					value = cost_of_carriers
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = gui_total_navy_cost
					value = cost_of_battleship
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = gui_total_navy_cost
					value = cost_of_heavy_cruiser
				}

					var = gui_total_navy_cost
					value = cost_of_light_cruiser
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = gui_total_navy_cost
					value = cost_of_destroyer

				}

				#TOTAL EXPENDITURES CALCULATIONS
				#Reset to 0 everytime
				set_variable = {
					var = gui_total_expenditures
					value = 0
				}
				#Military Service Cost
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_idea = volunteer_only
					}
					set_variable = {
						var = gui_military_service_cost
						value = 25
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = gui_total_expenditures
						value = 25
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_idea = limited_conscription
					}
					set_variable = {

						value = 50
					}

	#RESEARCH SPENDING TOP BAR
	research_spending_top_bar = {
		window_name = research_spending_top_bar
		
		context_type = player
		parent_window_token = top_bar

		research_spending_icon_click = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { show_research_design_tab_main = 0 }
				}
				set_variable = { show_research_design_tab_main = 1 }
				else = {
					set_variable = { show_research_design_tab_main = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		research_spending_bg_click = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { show_research_design_tab_main = 0 }
				}
				set_variable = { show_research_design_tab_main = 1 }
				else = {
					set_variable = { show_research_design_tab_main = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#BUDGET WINDOW
	budget_tab = {
		window_name = budget_tab_main
		context_type = player
		visible = {
			check_variable = { show_budget_tab = 1 }
		}

		effects = {
			increase_taxes_click = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = budget
					value = 1000
				}
			}

			decrease_taxes_click = {
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = budget
					value = 1000
				}
			}

			open_military_contract_menu_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 0 }
					}
					set_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 1 }
					else = {
						set_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 0 }
					}
				}
			}

			exit_button_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { show_budget_tab = 1 }
					}
					set_variable = { show_budget_tab = 0 }
					else = {
						set_variable = { show_budget_tab = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#MILITARY CONTRACTS WINDOW
	budget_military_contracts = {
		window_name = budget_military_contracts_tab_main
		context_type = player

		visible = {
			check_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 1 }
		}

		effects = {
			increase_inf_eq_number_click = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = inf_eq_order_amount
					value = 1000
				}
			}
			decrease_inf_eq_number_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { inf_eq_order_amount < 1 }
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = {
							var = inf_eq_order_amount
							value = 1000
						}
					}
				}
			}
			increase_inf_eq_number_shift_click = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = inf_eq_order_amount
					value = 10000
				}
			}
			decrease_inf_eq_number_shift_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { inf_eq_order_amount < 1 }
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = {
							var = inf_eq_order_amount
							value = 10000
						}
					}
				}
			}

			increase_h_inf_eq_number_click = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = h_inf_eq_order_amount
					value = 500
				}
			}
			decrease_h_inf_eq_number_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { h_inf_eq_order_amount < 1 }
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = {
							var = h_inf_eq_order_amount

						}
					}
				}
			}

			increase_support_eq_number_click = {

					var = support_eq_order_amount
					value = 500
				}
			}
			decrease_support_eq_number_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { support_eq_order_amount < 1 }
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = {
							var = support_eq_order_amount
							value = 500
						}
					}
				}
			}

			infantry_buy_click = {
				set_country_flag = infantry_equipment_order_1
				country_event = { id = ATOM_military_contracts.1 }
			}

			h_infantry_buy_click = {
				set_country_flag = infantry_equipment_order_2
				country_event = { id = ATOM_military_contracts.2 }
			}

			support_buy_click = {
				set_country_flag = infantry_equipment_order_3
				country_event = { id = ATOM_military_contracts.3 }
			}


			research_a_thing_click = {

				# 	}

			}
			
			exit_button_click = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 1 }
					}
					set_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 0 }
					else = {
						set_variable = { show_budget_tab_military_contracts = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
